Following a road deep within the plains. (road). (Bardosi Plains.) Black leather catching your eye, a rough battle-worn saddle has been left here. Tongue lolling from a bleeding maw, this grey wolf has been savagely killed. The shining figure of a Seraphic guardian floats in the air here. Komatata Anar-Alurl, Seraphic Pride is here, shrouded. He wields a spiritual mace in his left hand and a tower shield in his right. You see exits leading southeast, southwest, and a stone road leads to the northeast and south.
